Browser extensions simply add features and functions to a browser. That's it. iiSnrV"><div data-testid="callout-conversion-panel" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 iiTDiY"><div direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jUioWV"><h4 data-testid="callout-conversion-panel-title" font-size="s28" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 jafAqy">What are web browser extensions?</h4><div data-testid="callout-conversion-panel-body" width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 sc-7ddf7a40-0 ktJgKx jEMXq">Browser extensions make your life easier by adding custom features to your web browser, whether you use <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.google.com/chrome/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Chrome</span></span></a></span>, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.apple.com/safari/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Safari</span></span></a></span>, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/edge" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Edge</span></span></a></span>, or <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.mozilla.org//firefox/browsers/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Firefox</span></span></a></span>. Think of extensions kind of like apps: They each add different functions so its faster to do tasks and connect with people.<br><br>A web extension can be a simpler way to use software you already own. Or, an extension can improve your web browsing with totally new features, like blocking pop-up ads, autofilling forms with your contact information, sending notifications, and so on.</div></div></div></div></div><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">If youve never used a browser extension before, no worries. If you can browse the internet and download apps, then you absolutely have the know-how to add a web browser extension. In fact, you may already use one and not even know it!</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Read on, and this post will clarify what browser extensions do, explain how to use them efficiently and safely, and give you examples of practical extensions to try first. (And weve thrown in a few good ones to get started with, just for fun.)</p><h4 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 fWbnVd"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-4d83bcfc-0 hgKOdK bnRkbO">Pro Tip</span></h4><blockquote class="sc-9f52a7fd-4 kSHreE"><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">For the average user, the terms extension, add-on, and add-in all basically mean the same thing: a piece of software that adds new features to your browsing experience. </p></blockquote><h2 id="Why-would-I-want-to-use-web-browser-extensions?&nbsp;" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">Why would I want to use web browser extensions?&nbsp;</h2><figure width="auto" height="auto" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iMfKlp"><div direction="column" data-testid="video-player-wistia" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 XJtmH"><div width="auto" direction="column" data-testid="component-video-player" display="flex" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-78c639b-0 jCLgiO ivIuXE"></div><div display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-78c639b-1 dYgRlu lJMtx"><div height="auto" width="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 eEXJEk"><div display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jbNABl"><div class="sc-a196fe79-0 dcfLXI wistia_responsive_wrapper" data-testid="wistia-embed" style="position:relative"><div class="wistia_video_foam_dummy" data-source-container-id="wistia-v6bfipcsjr-1" style="border: 0px; #wistia_grid_43_below{position:relative;}</style></div></div></div><div style="pointer-events: none; opacity: 0; visibility: hidden; height: 100%; width: 100%; aspect-ratio: 1 / 0.562501;"></div></div></div></div></div></div></figure><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">The whole idea behind browser extensions is simple.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Like browser bookmarks, browser extensions are easy to access (one click!), but more powerful  they bring additional features to the forefront of the tab you're already working in. Instead of opening software in a new browser tab or app, you can access the app from your current tab.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://hbr.org/2022/08/how-much-time-and-energy-do-we-waste-toggling-between-applications" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Studies prove we lose a lot more time than we realize</span></span></a></span> jumping back-and-forth between tabs and apps. Its common by the end of the day to have dozens of tabs open and still not be able to find what youre looking for (or remember why you opened a specific tab in the first place).&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Browser extensions are the quickest way to use multiple types of software without interrupting your workflow.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Lets say you write in <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.google.com/docs/about/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Google Docs</span></span></a></span>, which offers basic help with grammar and spelling. You also may use a tool called <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.grammarly.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Grammarly</span></span></a></span>, an AI writing assistant that makes more advanced edits for tone, clarity, and vocabulary.</p><figure direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kcNCVO"><div data-testid="image" title="Screenshot showing how Grammarly's extension can pop up when you need it, and work for you without making you leave your document." class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 bhbaoe ezMOoT next-image-wrapper" display="flex" width="100%"><img data-testid="image" alt="Screenshot showing how Grammarly's extension can pop up when you need it, and work for you without making you leave your document." loading="lazy" width="1369" height="1152" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/4DcuAZcNRoFihRvsqPgytb/639cc0611dd7799d2a00da1f64a3f6d9/Grammarly_Google_Docs_extension.png?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div><div height="auto" width="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 jJotaI"><figcaption class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 bTrDZA">Here you can see how Grammarly's extension can pop up when you need it, and work for you without making you leave your document and opening a new tab. Image courtesy Grammarly</figcaption></div></figure><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Many people want the features of both tools. But its a pain to have two separate tabs open, copy-and-paste your text into Grammarly, and lose most of your document formatting.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Instead, you can just add the <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://support.grammarly.com/hc/en-us/articles/21227721882253-Introducing-app-actions" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Grammarly extension</span></span></a></span> to your web browser. Each web browser has an online store where you can install free or paid extensions in just a few clicks. For example, to add a Chrome Grammarly extension, all you need to do is find the listing in the <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://chromewebstore.google.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Chrome Web Store</span></span></a></span>, click "Add to Chrome," and confirm you want to install the extension. You can find your installed extensions by clicking the puzzle piece-shaped icon in your browser's navigation bar.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Once you have the Grammarly extension installed, then you can stay in Google Docs, click a button on your web browser, and Grammarly will do its magic right inside your document. No cutting-and-pasting. No losing formatting. No time wasted.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">If that sounds like you get to have your cake and eat it too, youre right.&nbsp;</p><h2 id="Are-web-browser-extensions-safe?&nbsp;" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">Are web browser extensions safe?&nbsp;</h2><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">The most popular browser extensions designed by trusted brands are generally safe. But as with everything on the internet, there are always a few neer-do-wells trying to access your devices in sneaky ways. Steer clear of malicious extensions by asking yourself these questions:</p><ul class="sc-9f52a7fd-1 buUria"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Are you downloading the extension from your browsers official extension site?</b> Here are links to the official online stores for extensions: <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://chromewebstore.google.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Chrome</span></span></a></span>, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.apple.com/app-store/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Safari</span></span></a></span> (the Apple App Store), <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://microsoftedge.microsoft.com/addons/Microsoft-Edge-Extensions-Home" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Edge</span></span></a></span>, and <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://addons.mozilla.org//firefox/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Firefox</span></span></a></span>. Its in the browser companys best interest to ensure the extensions they promote are secure, and take down anything they get complaints about.&nbsp;</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Is the developer trustworthy?</b> For example, if a well-known brand like <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://chromewebstore.google.com/detail/tripadvisor-browser-butto/oiekdmlabennjdpgimlcpmphdjphlcha" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Tripadvisor</span></span></a></span> builds an official browser extension, they likely have the resources to monitor and improve the tool for the long haul.&nbsp;</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">When was the last time the extension was updated?</b> Newer, consistently updated tools are more secure than old, out-of-date tools.</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Do you see any odd or unreasonable requests for personal information?</b> If youre installing a password keeper extension, it makes sense the developer would ask for some authentication. But if youre downloading a just-for-fun extension that turns your cursor into a duck, that company shouldnt need your date of birth and mothers maiden name.&nbsp;</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Does the developer clearly state what theyll do with your info?</b> Heres a good <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://explore.zoom.us/docs/ent/privacy-and-security.html#:~:text=Zoom%20takes%20your%20privacy%20extremely,ensure%20it%20is%20delivered%20effectively." rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">security and privacy example from Zoom</span></span></a></span> that explains what info they store, if they sell your data to third parties, etc.&nbsp;</p></li></ul><figure direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kcNCVO"><div data-testid="image" title="Screenshot of Microsoft Edges Add-Ons store, which is one example of an official marketplace to download safe browser extensions." class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 bhbaoe ezMOoT next-image-wrapper" display="flex" width="100%"><img data-testid="image" alt="Screenshot of Microsoft Edges Add-Ons store, which is one example of an official marketplace to download safe browser extensions." loading="lazy" width="1364" height="1222" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/VcqBLE4ZvP4U7rxojDdsY/cedd699720bead20cff1ef965ef69d63/Edge_Add_On_Store_Screenshot.png?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div><div height="auto" width="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 jJotaI"><figcaption class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 bTrDZA">Play it safe by downloading browser extensions from official marketplaces like the Edge Add-Ons store. Image courtesy Microsoft</figcaption></div></figure><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">New extensions created by unfamiliar developers still can be hugely helpful and secure. Just be a little more careful before you install them. Look for some reviews about the extension and/or the developer. You can bank on it: If folks come across a scam or bad product online, they're generally quick to issue warnings in reviews and other public forums. And if you see any installed extensions that you don't remember adding, uninstall them ASAP.</p><h4 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 fWbnVd"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-4d83bcfc-0 hgKOdK bnRkbO">Pro Tip</span></h4><blockquote class="sc-9f52a7fd-4 kSHreE"><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Most web browser extensions are free, because software companies want you to use their software as much as possible. However, some developers ask for contributions or charge for extensions because they solve unique problems. Just like when you download apps on your phone, a small, one-off fee or annual charge is common with browser extensions like ad blockers, distraction removers, password keepers, and games. </p></blockquote><h2 id="Examples-of-popular-browser-extensions-and-what-they-do" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">Examples of popular browser extensions and what they do</h2><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">For your first foray into web browser extensions, we recommend starting with these popular, easy-to-use options.</p><h3 id="1.-Grammarly" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">1. Grammarly</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Overview:</b> <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.grammarly.com/browser" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Grammarly</span></span></a></span> analyzes your sentences as you write and adds color-coded underlines to words and phrases where you can improve your writing. You can apply Grammarlys suggestion with a single click, or expand the suggestion to learn more about it.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Main browser extension benefits: </b>Provides real-time writing suggestions in email, documents, social media, and pretty much everywhere else you write online. No more copying-and-pasting text from one tool to another and back again, which often results in lost formatting and increases your margin for error.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Availability:</b> Chrome, Safari, Edge, and Firefox</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Cost:</b> Free with a Grammarly account</p><figure direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kcNCVO"><div data-testid="image" title="Screenshot showing how Grammarly for Chrome provides real-time writing suggestions in a Microsoft Outlook email." class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 bhbaoe ezMOoT next-image-wrapper" display="flex" width="100%"><img data-testid="image" alt="Screenshot showing how Grammarly for Chrome provides real-time writing suggestions in a Microsoft Outlook email." loading="lazy" width="768" height="677" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/4OaAb0jieOQ8iJVjv1quXf/f216bd97f65943ef3a4f54ed46832da6/Grammarly_extension_for_Microsoft.png?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div><div height="auto" width="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 jJotaI"><figcaption class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 bTrDZA">Grammarly for Chrome provides real-time writing suggestions in email, Google Docs, LinkedIn, and nearly everywhere else you write online. Image courtesy Grammarly</figcaption></div></figure><h3 id="2.-Loom" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">2. Loom</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Overview:</b> <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://chromewebstore.google.com/detail/loom-%E2%80%93-screen-recorder-sc/liecbddmkiiihnedobmlmillhodjkdmb" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Loom</span></span></a></span> lets you record your web screen, voice, and face to create an instantly shareable video in less time than it takes to type an email. The tool is infinitely useful, especially when youre making a how-to video, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/online-collaboration-tools"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">collaborating with remote co-workers</span></span></a></span> in different time zones, and giving feedback and kudos, where tone and facial expressions are important.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Main browser extension benefits: </b>Whatever web page or spreadsheet or slides youre on, you can stay there. Make quick, easy recordings directly in your web browser with two clicks. The extension records your voice and lets you choose between three capture modes: screen only, camera only, and screen and camera together.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Availability:</b> Chrome</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Cost:</b> Free with a Loom account</p><figure direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kcNCVO"><div data-testid="image" title="Screenshot demonstrating how Loom's extension records your screen and camera together, from wherever you are on your screen." class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 bhbaoe ezMOoT next-image-wrapper" display="flex" width="100%"><img data-testid="image" alt="Screenshot demonstrating how Loom's extension records your screen and camera together, from wherever you are on your screen." loading="lazy" width="1174" height="948" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/3DOMHEULxqbT1XHYFpHXXO/3e99b2634211257f7f072e718f75770f/Loom_extension.jpeg?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div><div height="auto" width="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 jJotaI"><figcaption class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 bTrDZA"> Loom's extension records your screen and camera together. Pause, rewind and edit your video while recording, and pick up where you left off with Live Rewind. Once youre done recording, Loom has a link ready to share. Image courtesy Loom</figcaption></div></figure><h3 id="3.-Google-Translate" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">3. Google Translate</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Overview:</b> When youre on a web page, just click the <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://chromewebstore.google.com/detail/google-translate/aapbdbdomjkkjkaonfhkkikfgjllcleb?hl=en-GB" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Google Translate</span></span></a></span> icon and it will translate the page you're visiting from its original language to your language. So far, the tool supports more than 130 languages.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Main browser extension benefits: </b>Speed and access to more information. The extension is so much easier to use than hunting on a web site for that business different language options (which are usually limited to a few pages and a handful of languages). Plus, if you select your preferred language once, you can set it and forget it.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Availability:</b> Chrome</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Cost:</b> Free with a Google account</p><figure direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kcNCVO"><div data-testid="image" title="Screenshot showing how the Google Translate web extension lets you highlight a section of text in a Google doc and click on the Translate icon to translate the copy to your language." class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 bhbaoe ezMOoT next-image-wrapper" display="flex" width="100%"><img data-testid="image" alt="Screenshot showing how the Google Translate web extension lets you highlight a section of text in a Google doc and click on the Translate icon to translate the copy to your language." loading="lazy" width="640" height="400" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/392MHM8OY28xrJynf6OnRP/9a9f1065eaba3764b9e21b146b0b8505/Google_Translate_extension.png?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div><div height="auto" width="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 jJotaI"><figcaption class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 bTrDZA">Google Translate lets you highlight a section of text and click on the Translate icon to translate the copy to your language. Or, translate the entire web page by clicking the translate icon on the browser toolbar. Image courtesy Google</figcaption></div></figure><h3 id="4.-Calendly" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">4. Calendly</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Overview: </b><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/features/browser-extensions"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly</span></span></a></span> takes the back-and-forth out of scheduling meetings, and helps with meeting prep and follow up. When youre in a web browser, Calendlys extension lets you get more done in less time.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Main browser extension benefits</b>: Calendlys extension is the quickest way to book meetings no matter where youre working. Use Calendly while youre on the web, without switching browser tabs or going to your calendar. It just takes one click to access your meeting types and availability.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Availability: </b>Chrome, Edge, and Firefox</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Cost:</b> Free with a <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/signup"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly account</span></span></a></span></p><div class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-9f52a7fd-5 kXCqii exBzUa button-container" width="100%" display="flex"><a data-testid="primary-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dCoJlx" href="/signup"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx">Try Calendly for free</span></a></div><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div direction="column" data-testid="callout-testimonial" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 hFlcTa"><h3 font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 eLJaNK"><!-- -->Great add-on to my workflow. Calendly saves countless hours booking meetings, and the extension saves more time by giving me my links at the click of a button.<!-- --></h3><div data-testid="callout-testimonial-person" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kXCqii"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iOpdhU"><p font-size="s20" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 fkEhjj">James Harman, Calendly user</p></div></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div data-testid="callout-switchback" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 iiTDiY"><div overflow="hidden" data-testid="callout-switchback-image" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 cqdiqK"><div width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 kvHEiz bTbbHj next-image-wrapper" display="flex"><img alt="Webinar: Getting Started with Calendly" loading="lazy" width="0" height="0" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/3KPypsOmC7UXzHuu9XOuBU/2c2735eafc5a8e4066d696427ca086ff/-Webinar-_Calendly_new_user_webinar.png?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div></div><div direction="column" width="100%" display="flex" class="sc-dd2631d-0 dhjnTZ"><div display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 bhbaoe"><h4 data-testid="callout-switchback-title" font-size="s28" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 jafAqy">Webinar: Getting started with Calendly</h4></div><div data-testid="callout-switchback-body" width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 sc-eaa94a81-0 eFMMXe bDJlSh">New to Calendly? Most of them are designed to simplify your daily tasks and help you work more efficiently. But there are also lots of browser extensions that only exist to bring silliness into your life, including:&nbsp;</p><ul class="sc-9f52a7fd-1 buUria"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/googlifier/lblbdlideidphhfofbpocigbkkhingfg" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Googlifier</span></span></a></span>: Add googly eyes to any photo in your browser window.&nbsp;</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV"><span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/cursor-cat/aeehekhncjhhmchjolinnihgdpapmljk/related" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Cursor Cat</span></span></a></span>: Turn your cursor into a cat that follows your scrolling and clicking and, well, acts like a cat. You can find your installed extensions in your web browsers toolbar. For example, on Chrome, the extension icon looks like a little puzzle piece. When you click that, a menu of all your extensions will appear.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">If there are extensions you use every day, you may want to pin them to your toolbar. Do this by clicking the thumbtack icon next to the extension name. This adds the extension's icon right next to your URL bar, so you can access the extension in just one click.</p></blockquote><h2 id="See-what-browser-extensions-can-do-for-you" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">See what browser extensions can do for you</h2><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">So now you know: Extensions turn your web browser into a Swiss Army knife.
